@pytest.mark.test_p0
def test_I2_8_6_1(indigo2_obj, request, requires_aosptestapp):
antenna = 1
# get the test case number from the test case function name
test_case_no = get_test_case_no_for_report(request)
test_case_no = test_case_no.strip("."+str(antenna))
logging.info(str(test_case_no))

# get current date and time for reference for logcat monitor lookup
d_date, d_time = indigo2_obj.get_current_datetime()
# Send the broadcast intent to execute the test activity from AOSPTestApp
testactivity = "WifiAntennaSelection"
indigo2_obj.run_apk_activity(_aosptest_activity + testactivity, "-e USER_ACTION_SELECT_ANTENNA " + str(antenna))
keyword= testactivity+":"+test_case_no+":"
ret_val, line = indigo2_obj.logcat_wait_keyword(keyword, d_date, d_time)
logging.info("ret_val = " + str(ret_val))
if ret_val == 0:
apk_return_value = indigo2_obj.logcat_getline_index(ret_val, line, -2, ":")
apk_return_value = apk_return_value.split(" ")[1]
logging.info("apk_return_value: " + apk_return_value)
